## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Create ASNOrder Instance] --> B[Initialize Private Attributes]
    B --> C[Call Persistable Constructor]
    C --> D[ASNOrder Object Ready]
    D --> E{Property Access}
    E -->|Getter| F[Return Private Attribute Value]
    E -->|Setter| G[Validate Input Type]
    G --> H{Value Changed?}
    H -->|Yes| I[Update Private Attribute]
    I --> J[Call add_dirty_field]
    J --> K[Return Self for Chaining]
    H -->|No| K
    D --> L[is_valid Method]
    L --> M{Check Required Fields}
    M -->|All Valid| N[Return True]
    M -->|Invalid| O[Return False]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Created: __init__()
    Created --> Valid: All required fields set
    Created --> Invalid: Missing required fields
    Valid --> Modified: Setter called with new value
    Modified --> Valid: add_dirty_field() called
    Invalid --> Valid: Required fields populated
    Valid --> [*]: is_valid() returns True
    Invalid --> [*]: is_valid() returns False
```
